  <script type="text/javascript">
    (function() {
        var contextPath = '/jira';
        var eventBuffer = [];

        function printDeprecatedMsg() {
            if (console && console.warn) {
                console.warn('DEPRECATED JS - contextPath global variable has been deprecated since 7.4.0. Use `wrm/context-path` module instead.');
            }
        }

        function sendEvent(analytics, postfix) {
            analytics.send({
                name: 'js.globals.contextPath.' + postfix
            });
        }

        function sendDeprecatedEvent(postfix) {
            try {
                var analytics = require('jira/analytics');
                if (eventBuffer.length) {
                    eventBuffer.forEach(function(value) {
                        sendEvent(analytics, value);
                    });
                    eventBuffer = [];
                }

                if (postfix) {
                    sendEvent(analytics, postfix);
                }
            } catch(ex) {
                eventBuffer.push(postfix);
                setTimeout(sendDeprecatedEvent, 1000);
            }
        }

        Object.defineProperty(window, 'contextPath', {
            get: function() {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('get');
                return contextPath;
            },
            set: function(value) {
                printDeprecatedMsg();
                sendDeprecatedEvent('set');
                contextPath = value;
            }
        });
    })();

</script>

                <div id="description-val" class="field-ignore-highlight"> 
                 <div class="user-content-block"> 
                  <p>Built on top of <a href="https://issues.apache.org/jira/browse/SOLR-2894" title="Implement distributed pivot faceting" class="issue-link" data-issue-key="SOLR-2894"><del>SOLR-2894</del></a>, this patch adds percentiles and averages to facets, pivot facets, and distributed pivot facets by making use of range facet internals. </p>

class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"selah\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Chris Russell\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13403331_verbose subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'28\\/Jun\\/12 18:22\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-06-28T18:22:50+0000\'\u003e28\\/Jun\\/12 18:22\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e   - \u003cspan class=\\\"redText subText\\\" title=\\\"Chris Russell - 28\\/Jun\\/12 18:29\\\"\u003eedited\u003c\\/span\u003e \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-body flooded\\\"\u003e\u003cp\u003eThis patch builds upon the distributed pivot facets introduced in \u003ca href=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/browse\\/SOLR-2894\\\" title=\\\"Implement distributed pivot faceting\\\" class=\\\"issue-link\\\" data-issue-key=\\\"SOLR-2894\\\"\u003e\u003cdel\u003eSOLR-2894\u003c\\/del\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e and adds the ability to request rudimentary percentiles when faceting.  The percentiles are calculated by using range facets to create \\\"buckets\\\" which divide up the field in question.  A range facet is done on each bucket to determine the number of documents whose value falls within that bucket.  An average value for each bucket is determined by averaging the upper and lower bound of that bucket.  The count of documents for each bucket as well as the bucket average are used when determining percentiles, with the bucket average being returned as the percentile value.  Thus the accuracy of the value is determined by bucket size.  Smaller buckets will yield more accurate values but will be more computationally intensive.  \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eThe choice to use buckets and have \\\"fuzzy\\\" values was made because 1) We were using query facets to do this already and desired a solution that involved less querying and 2) Our use case involves document counts on the order of tens of millions and distributed coalescing distinct values during distributed search seemed problematic from a performance standpoint.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eUsage:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  Querying:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  Faceting must be enabled (facet=true).  Then you may use the following parameters to define your percentiles request:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles=true : enables facet statistics\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles.field=fieldname : field to calculate facets for; can be specified more than once\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles.requested.percentiles=25,50,75 : requested percentiles i.e. 25th,50th,75th\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles.lower.fence=0 : lower bound for percentiles calculation i.e. lower edge of first bucket\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles.upper.fence=5000 : upper bound for percentiles calculation i.e. upper edge of last bucket\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles.gap=10 : bucket size i.e. bucket1 0-10, bucket2 10-20, etc (double counting on edges avoided similar to range facets)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  percentiles.averages=true : set this if you would like average and doc count reported for each field (average is weighted average of bucket midpoints)\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  facet.pivot=field1,field2 : if you ask for pivots, percentiles will show up on a per-pivot basis!\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eHere is an example URL using the example documents included with solr:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\u003ca href=\\\"http:\\/\\/localhost:8983\\/solr\\/select?q=*%3A*&amp;start=0&amp;rows=3&amp;wt=xml&amp;facet=true&amp;percentiles=true&amp;percentiles.field=popularity&amp;percentiles.requested.percentiles=25,50,75&amp;percentiles.averages=true&amp;facet.field=price&amp;facet.field=popularity&amp;facet.pivot=manufacturedate_dt&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.lower.fence=0&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.upper.fence=11&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.gap=1&amp;facet.sort=index&amp;percentiles.field=price&amp;percentiles.lower.fence=0&amp;percentiles.upper.fence=5000&amp;percentiles.gap=10\\\" class=\\\"external-link\\\" rel=\\\"nofollow\\\"\u003ehttp:\\/\\/localhost:8983\\/solr\\/select?q=*%3A*&amp;start=0&amp;rows=3&amp;wt=xml&amp;facet=true&amp;percentiles=true&amp;percentiles.field=popularity&amp;percentiles.requested.percentiles=25,50,75&amp;percentiles.averages=true&amp;facet.field=price&amp;facet.field=popularity&amp;facet.pivot=manufacturedate_dt&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.lower.fence=0&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.upper.fence=11&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.gap=1&amp;facet.sort=index&amp;percentiles.field=price&amp;percentiles.lower.fence=0&amp;percentiles.upper.fence=5000&amp;percentiles.gap=10\u003c\\/a\u003e  \u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eResults format:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  If percentiles are requested the \\\"facet_statistics\\\" node will show under \\\"facet_counts\\\". Each field requested will have its own subsection.  Each subsection will contain percentiles and optionally average and count.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  If pivot facets are also requested, each level of pivot will have a \\\"statistics\\\" section that will contain per-field info similar to that found in \\\"facet_statistics\\\" above.\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n\\n\u003cp\u003eNotes:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  All field types that range facets support are supported, however average on a date field will always return as 0. Apologies.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  Works in distributed mode!\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  Includes a unit test.\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n  If you\'re curious about what settings are used internally for the range faceting, it is:\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n    \\trangeHardEnd = false;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\tincludeLower = true;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\tincludeUpper = false;\u003cbr\\/\u003e\\n\\tincludeEdge = false;\u003c\\/p\u003e\\n \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003cdiv class=\\\"twixi-wrap concise actionContainer\\\"\u003e\\n        \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-head\\\"\u003e\\n            \u003ca href=\\\"#\\\" title=\\\"Expand comment\\\" class=\\\"twixi\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"icon-default aui-icon aui-icon-small aui-iconfont-collapsed\\\"\u003e\u003cspan\u003eShow\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n            \u003cdiv class=\\\"action-details flooded\\\"\u003e\\n                        \\n    \\n    \\n                                            \\n    \\n                \\n\\n    \u003ca class=\\\"user-hover user-avatar\\\" rel=\\\"selah\\\" id=\\\"commentauthor_13403331_concise\\\" href=\\\"\\/jira\\/secure\\/ViewProfile.jspa?name=selah\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar aui-avatar-xsmall\\\"\u003e\u003cspan class=\\\"aui-avatar-inner\\\"\u003e\u003cimg src=\\\"https:\\/\\/issues.apache.org\\/jira\\/secure\\/useravatar?size=xsmall&amp;avatarId=10452\\\" alt=\\\"selah\\\" \\/\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e Chris Russell\u003c\\/a\u003e\\n added a comment  - \u003cspan class=\'commentdate_13403331_concise subText\'\u003e\u003cspan class=\'date user-tz\' title=\'28\\/Jun\\/12 18:22\'\u003e\u003ctime class=\'livestamp\' datetime=\'2012-06-28T18:22:50+0000\'\u003e28\\/Jun\\/12 18:22\u003c\\/time\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e\u003c\\/span\u003e   - \u003cspan class=\\\"redText subText\\\" title=\\\"Chris Russell - 28\\/Jun\\/12 18:29\\\"\u003eedited\u003c\\/span\u003e                   This patch builds upon the distributed pivot facets introduced in   SOLR-2894   and adds the ability to request rudimentary percentiles when faceting.  The percentiles are calculated by using range facets to create \\\"buckets\\\" which divide up the field in question.  A range facet is done on each bucket to determine the number of documents whose value falls within that bucket.  An average value for each bucket is determined by averaging the upper and lower bound of that bucket.  The count of documents for each bucket as well as the bucket average are used when determining percentiles, with the bucket average being returned as the percentile value.  Thus the accuracy of the value is determined by bucket size.  Smaller buckets will yield more accurate values but will be more computationally intensive.   \\n\\n The choice to use buckets and have \\\"fuzzy\\\" values was made because 1) We were using query facets to do this already and desired a solution that involved less querying and 2) Our use case involves document counts on the order of tens of millions and distributed coalescing distinct values during distributed search seemed problematic from a performance standpoint. \\n\\n Usage: \\n  Querying: \\n  Faceting must be enabled (facet=true).  Then you may use the following parameters to define your percentiles request: \\n  percentiles=true : enables facet statistics \\n  percentiles.field=fieldname : field to calculate facets for; can be specified more than once \\n  percentiles.requested.percentiles=25,50,75 : requested percentiles i.e. 25th,50th,75th \\n  percentiles.lower.fence=0 : lower bound for percentiles calculation i.e. lower edge of first bucket \\n  percentiles.upper.fence=5000 : upper bound for percentiles calculation i.e. upper edge of last bucket \\n  percentiles.gap=10 : bucket size i.e. bucket1 0-10, bucket2 10-20, etc (double counting on edges avoided similar to range facets) \\n  percentiles.averages=true : set this if you would like average and doc count reported for each field (average is weighted average of bucket midpoints) \\n  facet.pivot=field1,field2 : if you ask for pivots, percentiles will show up on a per-pivot basis! \\n\\n Here is an example URL using the example documents included with solr: \\n http:\\/\\/localhost:8983\\/solr\\/select?q=*%3A*&amp;start=0&amp;rows=3&amp;wt=xml&amp;facet=true&amp;percentiles=true&amp;percentiles.field=popularity&amp;percentiles.requested.percentiles=25,50,75&amp;percentiles.averages=true&amp;facet.field=price&amp;facet.field=popularity&amp;facet.pivot=manufacturedate_dt&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.lower.fence=0&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.upper.fence=11&amp;f.popularity.percentiles.gap=1&amp;facet.sort=index&amp;percentiles.field=price&amp;percentiles.lower.fence=0&amp;percentiles.upper.fence=5000&amp;percentiles.gap=10    \\n\\n Results format: \\n  If percentiles are requested the \\\"facet_statistics\\\" node will show under \\\"facet_counts\\\". Each field requested will have its own subsection.  Each subsection will contain percentiles and optionally average and count. \\n  If pivot facets are also requested, each level of pivot will have a \\\"statistics\\\" section that will contain per-field info similar to that found in \\\"facet_statistics\\\" above. \\n\\n Notes: \\n  All field types that range facets support are supported, however average on a date field will always return as 0. Apologies. \\n  Works in distributed mode! \\n  Includes a unit test. \\n  If you\'re curious about what settings are used internally for the range faceting, it is: \\n    \\trangeHardEnd = false; \\n\\tincludeLower = true; \\n\\tincludeUpper = false; \\n\\tincludeEdge = false; \\n             \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n        \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n    \u003c\\/div\u003e\\n\u003c\\/div\u003e\\n My vote is to move this into a more modular component until things settle down. \\n\\n Please let me know if this is way off - also what the process would be to re-integrate - since this a module like carrot and others, I\'d imagine it would be (at least in the beginning) for people to adopt by modifying their solr config and downloading the JAR. \\n\\n In any case - roadmap is to support range, distributed, and more block join fun.
